As consequence, this deck also holds Tolarian Academy as flavored land to untap and Treasure Trove to draw before opponent's end of turn.

Without considering the combo with Juzam Djinn and the other creatures, this deck allows a free use of Ashes to Ashes and Hellfire, without suffering any damage.
Manalink3/Mods/PlayDeck/Degenerate/Orion79 themed/Landfall Deck.dck:8:memory-allocation:;Landfall ability grant some extra benefits whenever a new land comes into play under owner's control. This deck enhances this process using Trade Routes to bounce lands back to hand and re-play them more than once in a turn with Exploration. Also, Lotus Cobra may help to obtain more mana than the one needed to bounce the lands, with outstanding results.
